loading Carcinogenic, Toxic or Bioaccumulative cargoes, spot checks of vapor concentrations should be carried out with Draeger tubes, to ascertain is TLV-TWA are being exceeded, and if PPE like face </span>on<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.05pt;\"> </span>deck.<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.05pt;\"> </span>E<span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.05pt;\">p</span>ichloro<span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.05pt;\">7</span>,<span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.05pt;\"> </span>Methanol<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.05pt;\"> </span>is<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.05pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.05pt;\">0</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.05pt;\">.</span>46<span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.05pt;\"> </span>(200/92)<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">PPE must make allowance for ergonomic demands<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Safety lamp must run for 3 hrs.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">PPE gloves and boots must electrically non conductive<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">When you do manifold duty wear face shield<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Filter protection must only be used against gases which has a distinctive smell and there is no lack of oxygen. If you can smell gas it means the filter is saturated and is to be discarded.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Class 1/ 1000ppm<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Class2/ 5000 ppm<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Mark X/ low BP products<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Filter masks can be used only 3hrs in a working day.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Turbo filters have a battery powered blower which reduces the work on the lungs.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Use harness not belt.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Air driven lamps. Air supply to be fitted with water traps. Supply hoses of low electrical resistance. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Non ferrous tools not recommended as the working face picks upharder particles which can cause sparks<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Undersides of aluminium gangways should be protected by wood/plastic so that they do not leave a smear on rusty steel which can produce an incendive spark.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Toxicity/ sometimes one vapor+ another can become toxic.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Depending on the health hazards on the MSDS sheet use eye goggles, face visor, gloves, chemical suit etc when engaged in cargo work, tankcleaning or handling chemicals.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Be familiar with eye wash and shower arrangements. Eye lids may have to be forced open for proper flushing.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Use splash couplings at the manifold for corrosive/ toxic cargoes.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Do not use SCBA apparatus before conducting the mandatory HP,LP and pressure drop test.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Be familiar with oxygen resuscitator test and guedel airway.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">There must be a culture that no sailor takes boiler suits and working shoes to his cabin.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Wash your hands well with soap before meals.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Do not enter the pumproom without informing OOW.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">All walkways and deck surfaces must be kept non slip at all times as a policy. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">When using MOT ladder the top end shall be securely lashed to the ship.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Shore personnel and visitors must not be allowed enrty in restricted areas without permission from duty officer. CCR is a restricted area.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">When seamen work aloft greater than 5 feet they must wear harness<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">No movement is allowed on deck without helmets and proper footwear.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Seamen shall wear appropriate safety gear like visor , chemical suit etc when working at manifold, stripping and other cargo operations.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Fill up the appropriate company check lists prior starting work.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Do not open any pipeline without depressurizing it first.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">When weather is bad follow heavy weather routine.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Crew must be aware of the direction of wind by looking at the anemometer fan on the mast during cargo operations.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">No women visitors are allowed ( unless for official purposes )without the permission of master or chief officer.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">At doubtful ports a full scale stowaway/ drug search shall be carried out prior sailing.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">During loaded passage seamen shall walk on the lee side of main deck to perevent getting injured or washed overboard by waves.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">At sea, the Framo power pack in the forecastle shall not be started unless authorized by chief officer. A flooded FP store will cause ship to go off hire.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The crane cannot be topped up at sea without the permission of Chief officer or Master. The hook must have 2 guide lines. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Those not actually involved in a job should still be aware of what is happening, so that they may avoid putting themselves at risk or interfere with an unsafe act before it is too late. All&nbsp; should care for their own health and safety and for their shipmates. Any serious or imminent danger should be reported immediately to an appropriate officer..<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The Master should ensure that every risk to health and safety of persons working aboard ship is properly evaluated. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Walkie-Talkies should be kept in a fully charged condition. Chemical men wear the walkie talkie on their collar bone, so that both hands are free and the speaker is close to the ear.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Leads to portable instruments should not pass through doors in watertight bulkheads or fire door openings when the ship is at sea.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Minor wounds, cuts and abrasions should be treated and dressed at once, for protection against infection.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">All must be familiar with eye wash and shower arrangements.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Prolonged exposure to chemicals and solvents may cause dermatitis and other serious skin disorders. All chemical traces should be thoroughly washed from the skin using soap and water. Barrier creams may help protect exposed skin and also make cleaning easier. Never wash your hands in solvents.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Working boilersuits should be laundered frequently in a dedicated washing machine.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Chemical soaked rags should never be put in pockets.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Accidental exposure to toxic chemicals should be reported immediately to a responsible officer for the appropriate remedial action.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Use proper face masks when sweeping health hazardous cargoes like yellow grease ( crushed bone meal ), tallow etc.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">High humidity and heat can lead to heat exhaustion and heat stroke which may be fatal. When working in these conditions during tankcleaning or in port, drink plenty of water in small amounts at frequent intervals. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Mis-use of alcohol affects a person's fitness for duty and harms his health. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 12.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\nSmoking is a practice not very welcome on chemical tankers. It affects work output.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">If a load appears too heavy for one man, arrange for assistance. When two or more men are handling a load, it is preferable that they should be of similar height. The actions of lifting, lowering and carrying should, as far as possible, be carried out in unison to prevent strain and overbalance by either person. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Suitable safety shoes should be worn to protect toes from crushing. Sometimes safety shoes can be useful to take the load, when lowering, to allow hands to be withdrawn from underneath , say a reducer. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Clothing should be reasonably close fitting to avoid snagging and also give protection. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The overalls and safety boots supplied on board the vessel are to be worn at all times when working . These garments are to be looked after and not modified in any way like hacking off sleeves etc. Long sleeves afford better protection and should not be rolled up.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Loose clothing, fingers rings and jewellery can be hazardous when working on chemical tankers. Long hair should also be covered.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">All personnel must wear the appropriate personal protective equipment. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Goggles&nbsp; of the appropriate type and as required are to be worn on top of hardhats by deck crew to be used when required at an instant notice. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The correct type of gloves are to be worn to provide protection to the hands. Always consider the type of work to be done and the most suitable gloves. Whilst loose fitting gloves allow hands to slip out quickly they do not allow for good grip when climbing ladders. Wet and oily gloves may be slippery and hazardous to use.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Instruction plates, notices and operating indicators should be kept clean and legible. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Doors, whether open or closed, should be properly secured and never left swinging. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Fire doors and appropriate water tight doors should always be left closed and not secured open.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">In carrying out a task, always consider possible related consequences eg; the danger of wash down&nbsp; spraying onto an electrical switch board.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Where appropriate, warning signs must be posted at tanks which are not safe to enter or is inerted with nitrogen. <a href=\"http://www.blogger.com/post-edit.g?blogID=3564735312144269387&amp;postID=7714590723000581696\" name=\"SA128\"><o:p></o:p></a></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">IMO Signs and symbols to be&nbsp; exhibited as required. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Walkway areas should have slip-resistant surfaces. Sand or some other suitable substance should be spread over an area made slippery by snow, ice or water. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Spillages of oil or grease etc., should be cleaned up as soon as possible.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Catwalk gratings shall be adequately maintained.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Permanent fittings which may cause obstruction and be dangerous should be made conspicuous by means of colouring or marking or lighting. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Broken or defective lights or water/ insect logged lights should be reported to the responsible officer and repaired as soon as practicable. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">AC on ships must no longer be under 100% recirc , due to vaccum being created by exhaust fans of Galley and sanitary space. The AC fresh air intake if fitted with Gas Detection/ Alarm system , can warn of HC vapour ingress.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Visitors are also&nbsp; subject to PPE requirements, of Safety helmet ( provided by ship ) and appropriate footwear and clothing. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Lights which are designed to have cage protection should be equipped accordingly.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Defective equipment shall be repaired immediately or locked away and tagged \"OUT OF SERVICE DO NOT USE\" to avoid accidental use. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Personal oxygen monitors are not intended to be oxygen test meters. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Prior to going on scheduled watch the BAC should be theoretically ZERO.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Emergency shower must be stencilled in bold letters.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Filter mask\u2014full face with nose cup to prevent fogging, inhalation and exhalation valve<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Gas suits have resistance tables Viton/ Chloroprene rubber/ PVC. Positive pressure inside the suits&nbsp; add to safety<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Splash suits \u2013for protection against liquid splashes \u2013polyamide fabric coated both sides with PVC. Hood with draw string to fit under the helmet. Front&nbsp; zipper must be protected by double flyfront.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Gangway notice</span></i><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Visitors are required to show identification<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Mobile phones and other electronic eqipment to be switched off<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Lighters and matches prohibited to be carried on board<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Even if shore has provided gangway it is&nbsp; ships responsibility to provide the gangway net.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt;\"><tt><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">Safety Officer </b>must be familiar with his duties and responsibilities including the requirement to make monthly inspections of areas of his vessel, investigate <b><u>all</u></b> accidents, minor injuries, dangerous occurrences etc.</span></tt><span class=\"MsoHyperlinkFollowed\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"> </span></span><tt><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The reports arising from these investigations are to be recorded in a dedicated log book held by the safety officer. The Safety Officer\u2019s report in the Monthly Safety Committee meeting must be an extract of his log book.</span></tt><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n<br />\n<tt><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Even seemingly minor accidents should be investigated. As a guidance, any entries in the Medical Log which state that treatment has been administered, should also be mentioned in the accident investigation log.<o:p></o:p></span></tt></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">THERE IS&nbsp; \u2018<b><i><u>ZERO TOLERANCE POLICY\u2019</u></i></b>&nbsp; &nbsp;NON ADHERENCE TO COMPANY INSTRUCTIONS REGARDING WEARING HELMETS, SAFETY SHOES,&nbsp; SAFETY BELTS AND SUITABLE&nbsp; PPE.&nbsp; IN ADDITION TO RISKING YOUR LIFE IN A FOOLISH MANNER, YOU WILL NOT RECEIVE ANY FINANCIAL COMPENSATION IN CASE OF INJURY.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">TANKCLEANING SAFETY<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">It is company policy NOT to allow Toluene spraying due to danger of static explosion</span><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The pre cleaning temp must be well below the FP. &nbsp;If it not possible avoid ignition source.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Flushing / recirc with tankcleaning chemicals &lt;60 C FP requires an inerted tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Never wash and steam a tank simultanelously\u2014static electricity is generated<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">If the tank is having cargo of FP&lt;55 deg C flush tank with water first and then strip the bottom dry. Then gas free till the conc of LEL is &lt;50% for SS ( 40% for coated tanks ) before washing .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">One chemical is incompatible with another when on mixing temp rises more than 25 deg C or a gas is evolved.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">You can spray Methanol with a Graco barrel pump at 15 kg pressure\u2014but never ever toluene (static explosion ). Too may sailors have died at sea this way.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">In a tank of 100 CUM use can use only 3.8 litres of toluene for steaming so as not to exceed the LEL, while you can use 9 litres of methanol<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">A<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"> </b>flammable vapour mixture should be suspected within the tank or at any of its openings after unloading a volatile flammable cargo, a non-volatile flammable cargo carried at a temperature above its flash point, or any cargo loaded into a tank that was not free of flammable vapour. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Harmful concentrations of vapour should be suspected in all such spaces after loading cargoes having a vapour inhalation hazard.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-outline-level: 1; text-align: justify;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Washing in a Non-Inert Atmosphere</span></i><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Under the terms of Chapter 11-2 of the SOLAS Convention, 'new' chemical tankers (as defined in the Convention) over 20,000 DWT whose tanks have contained flammable chemicals can only be washed in a non-inert atmosphere if all the following conditions are met:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Individual tank capacity is less than 3000m3<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: -1.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Tank washing machine capacity per nozzle does not exceed 17.5,m3per hour; \u2013this means a&nbsp; twin nozzle machine shall not exceed 35m3/hour.and \u2013<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: -1.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Total combined washing machine throughout in the tank is less than 110m3 per hour.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: -1.0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Portable washing machines which are not in use shall be removed from the tank<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">These conditions have been introduced in order to minimise the risk of fire and explosion resulting from the generation and discharge of hazardous levels of static electricity: it is therefore recommended that 'new' chemical tankers of below 20,000 tonnes DWT and existing chemical tankers of all sizes also comply with them.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">If the cargo tank has been ventilated before washing to reduce the vapour concentration of the atmosphere to 10% or less of the LFL, the following procedures should be adopted in addition to the precautions set out previously:-<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Before washing, the tank bottom should be flushed with water and stripped. The piping system, including cargo pumps, crossover and discharge lines, should also be flushed with water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-list: skip; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-list: skip; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The flushing water should be drained to the tank designed or designated as a slop tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-list: skip; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-list: skip; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;This operation may not be necessary if the ship is fitted with an efficient stripping system and thecargo tank and pipelines have been stripped as detailed in the ship's procedures and arrangements manual.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-list: skip; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-list: skip; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Note</span></i><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">: If cargoes are highly water reactive this operation must not be carried out.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-list: skip; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Wash water may be heated, but if its temperature is above 60</span><span style=\"font-family: Symbol; font-size: 12pt;\">\u00b0</span><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">C, washing should be discontinued if the gas concentration reaches 35% of the LFL,<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-list: skip; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Small quantities of chemical additives may be used. Follow instructions on chemical additive MSDS instruction sheets.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-list: skip; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.25in;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">A<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"> </b>record should be kept showing the date and result of electrical continuity testing. Any hoses not meeting electrical continuity should be properly marked and taken out of service.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Washing machines should be suspended within a cargo tank by means of a natural fibre rope, and not by the water supply hose unless the manufacturer's instructions indicate otherwise.<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </b></span><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">All chemicals used for tank cleaning purposes (low and high flash solvents, detergents, emulsifiers or synthetic soaps) may generate electrostatic charges if allowed to free-fall or when sprayed.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Tank cleaning chemicals should therefore only be used to wash cargo tanks that are in a non-flammable condition.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Solvents may be used to clean tank walls in a localised area (e.g. wiping down) provided the amount of tank cleaning chemical is small and the personnel entering the tank observe all enclosed space entry requirements and wear the necessary protective clothing.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">In addition to the above, any manufacturers' instructions or recommendations for the use of these products should be observed and the resulting slops disposed of in accordance with the ship's Procedures and Arrangements Manual.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Where these operations take place in port, additional requirements may be imposed by local authorities.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Chlorinated solvent spraying is not permitted<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">No tankcleaning chemicals with cat Z&nbsp; components can be used unless they are readily biodegradable and present in a total concentration less than 10%<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p>BE SAFE-- YOU OWE IT TO YOUR FAMILY! &nbsp;COMPANY WILL GET INSURANCE FOR LOST HARDWARE.</o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRiUBd2WBhI/AAAAAAAACb8/C8x5X2fKV_c/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p>CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )</o:p></span></div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "1", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/7714590723000581696/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "4815603327119687969", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-06-01T00:12:00+05:30", "updated": "2011-12-06T13:28:55+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzIzMTU4MzM1MTY4Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/05/incompatibility-risks-on-parcel_31.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/4815603327119687969", "title": "INCOMPATIBILITY RISKS ON PARCEL CHEMICAL TANKERS--  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; font-size: 10pt;\"></span></span><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; External heating may cause an explosion<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Spontaneously flammable in air<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Fire from exothermic reaction-ignition of products or reactants<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Flammable gas generation<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Flammable, toxic gas generation; causes pressurization<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Heat generation by chemical reaction, may cause pressurization<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Dangerous heat generation due to heat of solution<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Violent polymerization, possibly with heat/toxic or flammable gas&nbsp;&nbsp; generation <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Can become highly flammable in use; causes pressurization<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Contact with substance liberates toxic gas; causes pressurization<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Innocuous and nonflammable gas generation; causes pressurization<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Contact with acids produces combustion enhancer (e.g., O2)<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Generates water soluble toxic products<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; May be hazardous but unknown<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Reaction may be intense or violent<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Possible exposure to radiation<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\"><br />\n</span> </span></div><div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">Stability During Transport</span></span></b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\"> - The term \"Stable\" means that the chemical will not decompose in a hazardous manner under the conditions of temperature, pressure, and mechanical shock that are normally encountered during shipment; the term does not apply to fire situations. Where there is a possibility of hazardous decomposition, an indication of the conditions and the nature of the hazard is given.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><o:p><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">CAPT <span class=\"goog-spellcheck-word\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">AJIT</span> <span class=\"goog-spellcheck-word\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">VADAKAYIL</span> ( 29 YEARS IN COMMAND )</span></o:p></div></div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "1", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/4815603327119687969/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "7539923922377085986", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-05-31T23:57:00+05:30", "updated": "2013-11-30T16:01:38+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzg1ODA3NDk4MTEwCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/05/nitrogen-generators-on-chemical-tankers.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/7539923922377085986", "title": "NITROGEN GENERATORS ON CHEMICAL TANKERS --  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRd0aYDTREI/AAAAAAAACa8/iRNjd-JtxHQ/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRd0aYDTREI/AAAAAAAACa8/iRNjd-JtxHQ/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\"><br />\n</span></b></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 16pt;\">PRESSURE SWING ADSORPTION - PSA / CARBON MOLECULAR SIEVE - CMS&nbsp;&nbsp;AND&nbsp;MEMBRANE NITROGEN GENERATOR PLANTS<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Pressure Swing Adsorption (PSA) is a process of separating molecules of gas from each other. It\u2019s not a chemical process, such as <i>\u201caBsorption\u201d,</i> rather it is physical process called \u201caDsorption. The first word is spelled using a \u201cB\u201d and the second is spelled using a \u201cD\u201d. This distinction helps you understand that a \u201cpressurized\u201d process, using carbon or zeolites, actually sifts molecules, which releases nitrogen from the air we breathe.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">The air we breathe is 78 percent nitrogen. This process separates it and the only waste product from the process is oxygen, which is sent back into the air. By forcing air into a pressure vessel or sieve-bed, filled with sieve, some molecules are trapped and others released. The captured nitrogen molecules are stored in a tank ready for use in the desired application.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></b><i><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">The&nbsp; \u201cmembrane\u201d process involves a series of hollow fibers that have holes in their walls. Compressed air is forced through the hollow fibers. The holes are small enough that nitrogen molecules are trapped. They are forced to escape. Heat is applied to excite the molecules in the hollow fiber to increase the chance they will permeate out through the holes. <o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">PSA process better suits \u201ccritical\u201d applications, while membrane is suitable for less critical requirements. When there is a need for high purity levels (up to 99.995) and low dewpoints, we often recommend a PSA system. The compressed air requirements are lower than the membrane systems and these systems are more tolerant to ambient temperature swings within a limited scope. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Between the PSA and membrane process for generating nitrogen, the answer is each meets special requirements, each has advantages and each has disadvantages. It takes a thorough understanding of the requirements to make the right choice. Some PSA systems may have a useful life of 20 years, <i>while some membrane systems may fail within 7 or 8 years.</i> <i><o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<i>Membranes are approximately 30% more expensive than PSA systems. &nbsp;They require more power than PSAs when operating at nitrogen purities of 98% and higher</i>. PSAs are more robust and less sensitive to hot and cold ambient conditions. <i>Membranes require 160 to 200 psig of compressed air for an efficient nitrogen separation to take place</i>. On the other hand, PSAs require a much lower air pressure to achieve an efficient separation<i>. Therefore, membranes will result in a higher outlet nitrogen pressure than PSA systems</i>. PSAs generally operate longer with less maintenance costs. <br />\n<br />\n<i>Membranes have fewer moving parts, but membranes begin to age and degrade over a relatively short period of time. Replacement of membrane modules, represent a significant capital cost to the buyer. The biggest advantage of membrane systems is their inherent lightweight and small footprint.<o:p></o:p></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\nThe carbon molecular sieve material used in PSA units is extruded from carbonized coconut shells and represents a very hard and durable form of carbon with an exceptionally high propensity for separating compressed air into pure nitrogen product. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<br />\nThe CMS material literally has an indefinite life. And like membrane fibers, it too requires protection from compressor oil carry-over. The filtration system in both the PSA and membrane unit is designed to prevent hydrocarbons from coming in contact with the CMS material and membrane fibers<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\nThe PSA system utilizes a programmable logic controller (PLC)&nbsp; to automatically control the operation of the Nitrogen Generator. This PLC consists of an 8k processor, power supply and I/O modules. The PLC performs all the controls and monitoring functions, including execution of the adsorption cycle. The PSA also has a built-in pressure switch and it monitors the nitrogen pressure. If no nitrogen is being used (or very little), the PSA will stop and go into standby mode. It will shut off the air inlet valve and nitrogen outlet valve so no air is used.<br />\n<br />\nThe air compressor also has a pressure switch or sensor that monitors downstream air pressure and it too, goes into a standby mode when the air pressure begins to rise. If the air compressor remains in this mode for more than three minutes, the main compressor motor will automatically shut down and wait until the air pressure is lowered before turning back on. This feature represents a tremendous power savings advantage. <br />\n<br />\n<i>The membrane system is totally reliant upon pressure switches to control its on and off operation. The pressure switch is installed in the nitrogen product line inside the control cabinet. The pressure switch can be set to turn the unit off and on at desired product pressure levels.<o:p></o:p></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<i><br />\n</i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\">\nA PSA Nitrogen Generator is a two-bed absorption system and therefore, has an interrupted air demand to the system when air is diverted from one bed to another. An air surge tank located downstream of the air compressor and upstream of the PSA unit is required in order to smooth out surges in air demand. <i>Membrane systems on the other hand, have a smooth constant demand for air and, otherwise do not necessarily require an air receiver.</i>. <br />\n<br />\nAgain, PSA systems require a nitrogen storage vessel in order to insure a smooth product delivery. <i>Membrane systems do not require as large a nitrogen storage vessel, but is still recommended to prevent the system from starting and stopping frequently.<o:p></o:p></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\">\n<i><br />\n</i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\">\nEvaporated liquid oxygen purity is 99.5% to 99.9% pure. Argon makes up about 4-5 percent of the oxygen product. After the compressed air leaves the air dryer, it is filtered in a series of filtration stages. The first and second stages consist of two acetate type filters with a pore space of 0.1 and 0.01 micron. These filters are designed primarily to remove water and particulates in the compressed air. The third and final stage is an activated carbon filter designed to eliminate any residual oil or hydrocarbon from the air before it passes into the adsorption vessels.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdz8-Q6cQI/AAAAAAAACa0/BQWgHgejbuY/s1600/psa.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdz8-Q6cQI/AAAAAAAACa0/BQWgHgejbuY/s1600/psa.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdz_zcFI1I/AAAAAAAACa4/X2MW1kETJuY/s1600/psa2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdz_zcFI1I/AAAAAAAACa4/X2MW1kETJuY/s400/psa2.jpg\" width=\"280\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;\">\n<b>PSA generators</b> These use carbon molecular sieve (CMS), which allows the smaller molecules in the input air (such as oxygen) to penetrate the CMS, whilst the larger molecules of nitrogen bypass the CMS to generate the output gas. A PSA generator consists of a pair of columns filled with CMS. PSA generators can achieve higher purity levels than membrane systems, up to 99.9995% <br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdz3aeu9qI/AAAAAAAACas/fgrwBRHBgFE/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"251\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdz3aeu9qI/AAAAAAAACas/fgrwBRHBgFE/s400/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdz6HPRimI/AAAAAAAACaw/3Z_0uVSqXgQ/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"229\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRdz6HPRimI/AAAAAAAACaw/3Z_0uVSqXgQ/s400/images.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<b><i>Membrane Generators</i></b><i>&nbsp; use a bundle of hollow fibres which separate gases by the principle of selective permeation. A membrane generator consists of these hollow fibres, encased within an outer shell of GRP. The faster permeating gases diffuse quickly through the membrane wall, leaving an output of nitrogen up to 99.9% pure. These systems are very compact and robust.<o:p></o:p></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\">\nPSA generators are less sensitive than membrane generators.&nbsp;They are more robust, thus more suitable for potentially harsh environments.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\">\n<i>Membrane generators seldom offer a purity higher than 99%.&nbsp;An optimal&nbsp;purity for membrane solutions is rarely&nbsp;higher than 94%.</i> This is not the case with PSA solutions. The gas purity from PSA generators is often 99.5% as standard - and can easily reach 99.9%.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<table border=\"0\" cellpadding=\"0\" cellspacing=\"0\" class=\"MsoNormalTable\" style=\"mso-cellspacing: 0in; mso-padding-alt: 0in 0in 0in 0in; mso-yfti-tbllook: 1184; width: 100.0%;\"><tbody>\n<tr>   <td style=\"padding: 0in 0in 0in 0in; width: 100.0%;\" valign=\"top\" width=\"100%\"></td>  </tr>\n</tbody></table>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\nEven at high volumes, PSA generators consistently produce the same high amount of gas. <i>By contrast, the capacity of membrane solutions tends to weaken over time<o:p></o:p></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\nOn average, maintenance costs for membrane solutions are 50% higher than for PSA solutions. This is due to the long lifespan of the pellets (Carbon Molecular Sieves) that form the hub of the PSA gas filtering process. The pellets can easily perform optimum separation for at least 10 years without being replaced. <i>By contrast, membranes are more fragile and start deteriorating&nbsp;from the moment the on-button is pressed. And membranes are&nbsp;expensive to replace.<o:p></o:p></i><br />\n<i><br /></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRd0n572oqI/AAAAAAAACbA/_uwBPwb4AOA/s1600/P4270001.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"200\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRd0n572oqI/AAAAAAAACbA/_uwBPwb4AOA/s200/P4270001.JPG\" width=\"185\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL &nbsp;( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. As a last resort I had held on to overhead pipes and used my feet on his torso from behind using my body weight \u2013in a type of Shaffer's style . The moment he started breathing we hooked on pure oxygen .<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">Since that incident he got promoted twice with NIL signs of brain damage.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">I would like to believe that went into a state of HIBERNATION or suspended animation or state of hypothermia -- triggered by some H2S gas just on top of the Palm oil derivative.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">My Russian Chief Engineer whose home was in the Ural mountains with plenty of bears would talk about how the bears love to bury freshly killed meat and wait till the carcass rotted before they would eat it, in the beginning of winter . I guess the whole thing is about Hydrogen Suphide which propels them into hibernation.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">Hydrogen sulfide is something all of us make in our bodies all the time to buffer our metabolic flexibility\u2014It is what makes our body core temperature to stay at 98.7 degrees F, regardless of whether we're in Siberia or Congo.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">Same way H<sub>2</sub>S is used by warm blooded animals, like bears that go into hibernation as a way of reducing body temperature .&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">The body temperature of a hibernating bear will drop from its usual 100 degrees F to 88 degrees F. The bear's heart will slow from 90 beats a minute down to 25 &nbsp;beats . Instead of its usual 18 &nbsp;breaths per minute, a hibernating bear will take one deep breath every 45 seconds.&nbsp;Electrical activity inside a hibernating &nbsp;brain indicates&nbsp;<a href=\"http://www.blogger.com/post-edit.g?blogID=3564735312144269387&amp;postID=8386599485803378889\" name=\"497408.hook\"></a>&nbsp;a 90 percent reduction .<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">The bear is &nbsp;balanced on a very narrow line between the maintenance of life at a level that makes recovery from hibernation possible and a reduction of metabolism to a level that will lead to death. Hibernation is entered into from a state of sleep.. Hibernation and sleep are somewhat similar in that essential body processes continue during both periods , though at a lowered level. .&nbsp;</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">E</span><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">xposed to food shortages, extremely low temperatures, the bear just turns off &nbsp;its thermostat and hibernates until the environment becomes more favourable. &nbsp;Lot of calories is requires to convert into heat and survive icy conditions.<o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TR9qCFgEHYI/AAAAAAAACiE/BSNc5UQn4H4/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TR9qCFgEHYI/AAAAAAAACiE/BSNc5UQn4H4/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">Hydrogen sulfide is similar to oxygen at the molecular level because it binds at many of the same proteins. As a result, H2S competes for and interferes with the body's ability to use oxygen for energy production -- a process within the cell's power-generating machinery called oxidative phosphorylation.&nbsp;During a hibernation-like state, cellular activity slows to a near standstill, which reduces dramatically the animals\u2019 need for oxygen.</span><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: 6.0pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">Hibernating animals conserve energy, during winter when food is short, tapping energy reserves,&nbsp;body fat, at a slow rate. It is the animal's slowed metabolic rate which leads to a reduction in body temperature and not the other way around.</span><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: 6.0pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: 5.45pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">As hibernation drastically reduces the amount of oxygen that cells need to survive It could be used to buy time when treating severe blood loss for wounded soldiers , hypothermia in freezing seas , &nbsp;heart attacks and strokes, in which oxygen deprivation kills off tissue, leading to disability or death.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: 5.45pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 12.9pt; margin-bottom: 4.55pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: #333333; font-size: 12pt;\">David Blaine was submerged in a water-filled sphere on the stage of \u201cThe Oprah Winfrey Show\u201d during a live broadcast, and he &nbsp;held his breath for 17 minutes and 4 seconds\u2014for a new &nbsp;Guinness World Record.
