It is an exciting period of discovery. Love will follow.<br />\n<br />\nOn the GRAPH of love versus time-- on X / Y axis, a love marriage starts at zero time ( wedding night ) on the horizontal axis and 100% love on the vertical axis.<br />\n<br />\nWhat is already on top cannot go up any more--remember you had been &nbsp;surviving on love and fresh air and showing only your best behavior and profile to each other , hiding all your warts, &nbsp;BO with perfume and MO with Wrigleys.<br />\n<br />\nWithin two months the index falls like an asymptotic curve.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-vvKmvZy5cM4/UmYGeEu_y1I/AAAAAAAAmiI/--WRzVgZWDw/s1600/asymptote-300x224.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-vvKmvZy5cM4/UmYGeEu_y1I/AAAAAAAAmiI/--WRzVgZWDw/s1600/asymptote-300x224.png\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nEverything in life is relative. In one , the index keeps falling , while in the other it has to rise.<br />\n<br />\nFor what was this love--just an arrangement of convenience.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-UV17uVp2kU8/VQwWrW-WMgI/AAAAAAAA2d4/LWqKjiRB-iI/s1600/loneliness-is-a-good-fee3BXling-when-it-is-creat-by-ourself.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"377\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-UV17uVp2kU8/VQwWrW-WMgI/AAAAAAAA2d4/LWqKjiRB-iI/s1600/loneliness-is-a-good-fee3BXling-when-it-is-creat-by-ourself.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIf you were staying in Mumbai you fall in love with a girl from Mumbai--if you were in Timbuctoo you fall in love with a girl from there. True love knows no barriers of race, religion or age.<br />\n<br />\nMy arranged marriage &nbsp;started with the index on zero love at zero time. What is already at rock bottom cannot fall any further. It can only go up. &nbsp;Ego does not play a huge role.<br />\n<br />\nMarriage is an institution which must be respected.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-J6cf0o0oczQ/VQwSeVMAqxI/AAAAAAAA2ds/QKSt4BCyTuU/s1600/imWCages.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"265\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-J6cf0o0oczQ/VQwSeVMAqxI/AAAAAAAA2ds/QKSt4BCyTuU/s1600/imWCages.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nI remember when my crew was Jamaican , and if they did something extraordinary , like winning a race at the Flying Angels athletic meet --<br />\n<br />\nI would pose a question. \" Brown , whom did you run for\" .<br />\n<br />\nPat comes the answer \" I ran for Maaamma \" .<br />\n<br />\nNaturally-- Brown did NOT run for Paaapa because his mother never married,-- she just lived in with lot of men.<br />\n<br />\ndigression:--<br />\n<br />\nHowever here is my self proclaimed answer to the first question --the first line of this piece. At our honeymoon hotel , they had a package for honeymoon couples. There were 12 newly weds in a nice luxury coach.<br />\n<br />\nOur first stop was the Ooty lake. All the eleven couples went for the foot paddle boats. I went for the rowing wooden boat with the heavy oars-- declined the services of a professional rower, and shot off to the other end of the huge lake like an arrow.<br />\n<br />\nVery soon i could see 11 envious ladies cajoling their husbands to be more &nbsp;romantic ( like me ) and row serenade them , &nbsp;instead of forcing them to use their delicate leg power.<br />\n<br />\n&nbsp;So we had 12 rowing boats in the lake -- pretty soon--with NO professional rowers in them.<br />\n<br />\nOut of these 12 , 11 got stuck in the slush with the grooms unable to row further due to enervated tendons &nbsp;fatigued muscles and blistered palms -- triggering off a huge rescue operation which took two hours, in front of a huge sniggering crowd.-- what with so much of smeared lipsticks and smudged mascaras--<br />\n<br />\nAll 11 genteel brides had panicked and were in tears--some of them wailing loudly.<br />\n<br />\nAll 11 grooms gave me dirty looks, for spoiling their party -- &nbsp;Their brides were giving me side glances of admiration.<br />\n<br />\nI could see that my wife was proud of me , for she started holding mE hand -- and she had reprogrammed her DNA to respect me for ever &nbsp;HA! &nbsp;;-).<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Below : This picture was taken immediately after the lake rowing incident- my nostrils are dilated and I am sweating and breathing hard -&nbsp;</b></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-hd3Psk85J_I/VQwDH9qogrI/AAAAAAAA2c8/RaVgux5TpyI/s1600/107.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-hd3Psk85J_I/VQwDH9qogrI/AAAAAAAA2c8/RaVgux5TpyI/s1600/107.jpg\" width=\"233\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nPSSST, secret -- &nbsp;Why should i tell her than i was a champion team rower of whaler and cutters while in our Training ship which had 250 cadets . We practised almost daily for 2 years. I used to be the bowman , who had 1:6 ratio on the crutch pivot while the rest of the team had 1:3 ( boat is narrow at the bows )<br />\n<br />\n--and my rowing tendons, were seasoned and tough -- like steel wires..<br />\n<br />\nTEEE--HEEEEEE !<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\">I have seen in Australia, &nbsp;police showing preferential treatment when the berserk drunken mob chasing Lebanese on the beachfront &nbsp;is made of English speaking whites. Another set of standards are shown for students of &nbsp;coloured Indian race who protest peacefully against racist violence , by pinning them down without escape routes--and not allowing them a voice.&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\">In the Jallianwala bagh massacre , the British had sealed off all escape routes before gunning down 1500 unarmed and peaceful people ( 10% of the crowd including women and children ) who were holding a meeting.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\">Ego laden Capt Bligh of Mutiny on the County fame could not see the signs of milling with a thousand natives beating rocks held in both hands together in unison on the beach -- causing painful loss of life .<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"background-color: white; color: black; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\">A crowd is not a mob but it can become one, in a jiffy&nbsp;\u2014 that all crowds can transform into law&nbsp;breaking mobs , is the core of mob sociology.&nbsp;&nbsp;A crowd is law abiding, while a mob is not.</span></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\">A crowd turns into a destructive mob only due to one factor-- ANONYMITY.</span></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; This is called mob mentality. &nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\"><br /></span></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Oof7nx9_4Fw/Ti_089zcRlI/AAAAAAAAEoE/WtfCykIgt5M/s1600/imagesCAT7MYX5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Oof7nx9_4Fw/Ti_089zcRlI/AAAAAAAAEoE/WtfCykIgt5M/s1600/imagesCAT7MYX5.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;verdana&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\">De individualisation leads to strange lowering of intellectual faculties and bizzare de-rationalisation.
